{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$template$<$ typename U, typename V, typename... Args $>$ class Object\+Type = std\+::map, template$<$ typename U, typename... Args $>$ class Array\+Type = std\+::vector, class String\+Type  = std\+::string, class Boolean\+Type  = bool, class Number\+Integer\+Type  = std\+::int64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Unsigned\+Type  = std\+::uint64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Float\+Type  = double, template$<$ typename U $>$ class Allocator\+Type = std\+::allocator, template$<$ typename T, typename SFINAE=void $>$ class JSONSerializer = adl\+\_\+serializer, class Binary\+Type  = std\+::vector$<$std\+::uint8\+\_\+t$>$$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::assert\+\_\+invariant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{check\+\_\+parents = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



checks the class invariants 

This function asserts the class invariants. It needs to be called at the end of every constructor to make sure that created objects respect the invariant. Furthermore, it has to be called each time the type of a JSON value is changed, because the invariant expresses a relationship between {\itshape m\+\_\+type} and {\itshape m\+\_\+value}.

Furthermore, the parent relation is checked for arrays and objects\+: If {\itshape check\+\_\+parents} true and the value is an array or object, then the container\textquotesingle{}s elements must have the current value as parent.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em check\+\_\+parents} & whether the parent relation should be checked. The value is true by default and should only be set to false during destruction of objects when the invariant does not need to hold. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

get a (pointer) value (explicit) 

Performs explicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value if required.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the requested type is a pointer to the internally stored JSON value that pointer is returned. No copies are made.
\item If the requested type is the current \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}, or a different \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json} convertible from the current \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}.
\item Otherwise the value is converted by calling the \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type\+CV} & the provided value type \\
\hline
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the JSON value, converted to 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & if necessary\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method throws if conversion is required\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

auto \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) -\/$>$ decltype(std\+::declval$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a125c0afa5f3599949b0589ef7b4aa322}{basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t}}\&$>$().template \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a85222410e03d8f5c8ff9c78cf9f6b1b6}{get\+\_\+ptr}}$<$Pointer\+Type$>$())     \hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



get a pointer value (explicit) 

Explicit pointer access to the internally stored JSON value. No copies are made.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The pointer becomes invalid if the underlying JSON object changes.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Pointer\+Type} & pointer type; must be a pointer to \doxylink{a01541_a858c1cf8407bc06494e3a1114a3b73e7}{array\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_aef3ff5a73597850597d1d40db9edd376}{object\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_a33593865ffb1860323dcbd52425b90c8}{string\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_a44fd1a12c9c54623c942b430e7a72937}{boolean\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_a11e390944da90db83089eb2426a749d3}{number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_ae09af9c23351b7245d9be4d1b2035fef}{number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}, or \doxylink{a01541_a5b8abaebd922d82d69756327c0c347e6}{number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to the internally stored JSON value if the requested pointer type {\itshape Pointer\+Type} fits to the JSON value; {\ttfamily nullptr} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
@complexity Constant.

@liveexample\{The example below shows how pointers to internal values of a JSON value can be requested. Note that no type conversions are made and a {\ttfamily nullptr} is returned if the value and the requested pointer type does not match.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Pointer\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \doxylink{a01541_a85222410e03d8f5c8ff9c78cf9f6b1b6}{get\+\_\+ptr()} for explicit pointer-\/member access
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

Value\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::get\+\_\+impl (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{a01249}{detail\+::priority\+\_\+tag}}$<$ 0 $>$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



get a value (explicit) 

Explicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value which is \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/CopyConstructible}{\texttt{ Copy\+Constructible}} and \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/DefaultConstructible}{\texttt{ Default\+Constructible}}. The value is converted by calling the \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method.

The function is equivalent to executing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{ValueType\ ret;}
\DoxyCodeLine{JSONSerializer<ValueType>::from\_json(*\textcolor{keyword}{this},\ ret);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ ret;}

\end{DoxyCode}


This overloads is chosen if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape Value\+Type} is not \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json},
\item \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} has a {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method of the form {\ttfamily void from\+\_\+json(const \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}\&, Value\+Type\&)}, and
\item \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} does not have a {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method of the form {\ttfamily Value\+Type from\+\_\+json(const \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}\&)}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the JSON value, converted to {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method throws\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
@liveexample\{The example below shows several conversions from JSON values to other types. There a few things to note\+: (1) Floating-\/point numbers can be converted to integers\textbackslash{}, (2) A JSON array can be converted to a standard {\ttfamily std\+::vector\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}short\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}\textbackslash{}, (3) A JSON object can be converted to C++ associative containers such as {\ttfamily std\+::unordered\+\_\+map\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}std\+::string\textbackslash{}, json\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Value\+Type\+\_\+const\}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

Args $>$ class Array\+Type = std\+::vector, class String\+Type  = std\+::string, class Boolean\+Type  = bool, class Number\+Integer\+Type  = std\+::int64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Unsigned\+Type  = std\+::uint64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Float\+Type  = double, template$<$ typename U $>$ class Allocator\+Type = std\+::allocator, template$<$ typename T, typename SFINAE=void $>$ class JSONSerializer = adl\+\_\+serializer, class Binary\+Type  = std\+::vector$<$std\+::uint8\+\_\+t$>$$>$ \\

Value\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::get\+\_\+impl (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{a01249}{detail\+::priority\+\_\+tag}}$<$ 1 $>$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



get a value (explicit); special case 

Explicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value which is {\bfseries{not}} \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/CopyConstructible}{\texttt{ Copy\+Constructible}} and {\bfseries{not}} \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/DefaultConstructible}{\texttt{ Default\+Constructible}}. The value is converted by calling the \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method.

The function is equivalent to executing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ JSONSerializer<ValueType>::from\_json(*\textcolor{keyword}{this});}

\end{DoxyCode}


This overloads is chosen if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape Value\+Type} is not \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json} and
\item \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} has a {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method of the form {\ttfamily Value\+Type from\+\_\+json(const \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}\&)}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} has both overloads of {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()}, this one is chosen.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the JSON value, converted to {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \doxylink{a01541_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method throws\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

Args $>$ class Array\+Type = std\+::vector, class String\+Type  = std\+::string, class Boolean\+Type  = bool, class Number\+Integer\+Type  = std\+::int64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Unsigned\+Type  = std\+::uint64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Float\+Type  = double, template$<$ typename U $>$ class Allocator\+Type = std\+::allocator, template$<$ typename T, typename SFINAE=void $>$ class JSONSerializer = adl\+\_\+serializer, class Binary\+Type  = std\+::vector$<$std\+::uint8\+\_\+t$>$$>$ \\
template$<$typename Pointer\+Type , \mbox{\hyperlink{a00662_a02bcbc878bee413f25b985ada771aa9c}{detail\+::enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$ Pointer\+Type $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a11641b35219676b225d9bd15c7677659}{\+::value}}, int $>$  = 0$>$ \\
constexpr auto \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::get\+\_\+impl (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{a01249}{detail\+::priority\+\_\+tag}}$<$ 4 $>$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const -\/$>$ decltype(std\+::declval$<$const \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a125c0afa5f3599949b0589ef7b4aa322}{basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t}}\&$>$().template \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a85222410e03d8f5c8ff9c78cf9f6b1b6}{get\+\_\+ptr}}$<$Pointer\+Type$>$())     \hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [constexpr]}, {\ttfamily [private]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



get a pointer value (explicit) 

get a pointer value (explicit)  

Explicit pointer access to the internally stored JSON value. No copies are made.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The pointer becomes invalid if the underlying JSON object changes.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Pointer\+Type} & pointer type; must be a pointer to \doxylink{a01541_a858c1cf8407bc06494e3a1114a3b73e7}{array\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_aef3ff5a73597850597d1d40db9edd376}{object\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_a33593865ffb1860323dcbd52425b90c8}{string\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_a44fd1a12c9c54623c942b430e7a72937}{boolean\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_a11e390944da90db83089eb2426a749d3}{number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{a01541_ae09af9c23351b7245d9be4d1b2035fef}{number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}, or \doxylink{a01541_a5b8abaebd922d82d69756327c0c347e6}{number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to the internally stored JSON value if the requested pointer type {\itshape Pointer\+Type} fits to the JSON value; {\ttfamily nullptr} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
@complexity Constant.

@liveexample\{The example below shows how pointers to internal values of a JSON value can be requested. Note that no type conversions are made and a {\ttfamily nullptr} is returned if the value and the requested pointer type does not match.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Pointer\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \doxylink{a01541_a85222410e03d8f5c8ff9c78cf9f6b1b6}{get\+\_\+ptr()} for explicit pointer-\/member access
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0   
\end{DoxySince}

helper function to implement \doxylink{a01541_a14ddc6e0f6d70296bc81f810254076c5}{get\+\_\+ref()} 

This function helps to implement \doxylink{a01541_a14ddc6e0f6d70296bc81f810254076c5}{get\+\_\+ref()} without code duplication for const and non-\/const overloads


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em This\+Type} & will be deduced as {\ttfamily \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}} or {\ttfamily const \doxylink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em type\+\_\+error.\+303} & if Reference\+Type does not match underlying value type of the current JSON \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{a00650__deprecated000002}{Deprecated}}]This function is deprecated since 3.\+1.\+0 and will be removed in version 4.\+0.\+0 of the library. {\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$template$<$ typename U, typename V, typename... Args $>$ class Object\+Type = std\+::map, template$<$ typename U, typename... Args $>$ class Array\+Type = std\+::vector, class String\+Type  = std\+::string, class Boolean\+Type  = bool, class Number\+Integer\+Type  = std\+::int64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Unsigned\+Type  = std\+::uint64\+\_\+t, class Number\+Float\+Type  = double, template$<$ typename U $>$ class Allocator\+Type = std\+::allocator, template$<$ typename T, typename SFINAE=void $>$ class JSONSerializer = adl\+\_\+serializer, class Binary\+Type  = std\+::vector$<$std\+::uint8\+\_\+t$>$$>$ \\
template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01333}{detail\+::conjunction}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01345}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$ Value\+Type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{a01345}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, \mbox{\hyperlink{a01221}{detail\+::json\+\_\+ref}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{basic\+\_\+json}} $>$ $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{a01345}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{a01345}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01289}{detail\+::is\+\_\+basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Value\+Type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{a01345}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, std\+::initializer\+\_\+list$<$ typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$ $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{a01273}{detail\+::is\+\_\+detected\+\_\+lazy}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a00662_ab4d22cdb6521ee3508db496dea66711e}{detail\+::get\+\_\+template\+\_\+function}}, const \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a125c0afa5f3599949b0589ef7b4aa322}{basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t}} \&, Value\+Type $>$ $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a11641b35219676b225d9bd15c7677659}{\+::value}}, int $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{a01541_a5b7c4b35a0ad9f97474912a08965d7ad}{\+::type}}  = 0$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{a00206_aefed8cf27cadeea45f12c6f3db3ce774}{JSON\+\_\+\+EXPLICIT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{a01541}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::operator Value\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



get a value (implicit) 

Implicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value. The call is realized by calling \doxylink{a01541_af1650e004db368459b3c0db041b32adc}{get() const}.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & non-\/pointer type compatible to the JSON value, for instance {\ttfamily int} for JSON integer numbers, {\ttfamily bool} for JSON booleans, or {\ttfamily std\+::vector} types for JSON arrays. The character type of \doxylink{a01541_a33593865ffb1860323dcbd52425b90c8}{string\+\_\+t} as well as an initializer list of this type is excluded to avoid ambiguities as these types implicitly convert to {\ttfamily std\+::string}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the JSON value, converted to type {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em type\+\_\+error.\+302} & in case passed type {\itshape Value\+Type} is incompatible to the JSON value type (e.\+g., the JSON value is of type boolean, but a string is requested); see example below\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
@complexity Linear in the size of the JSON value.

@liveexample\{The example below shows several conversions from JSON values to other types. There a few things to note\+: (1) Floating-\/point numbers can be converted to integers\textbackslash{}, (2) A JSON array can be converted to a standard {\ttfamily std\+::vector\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}short\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}\textbackslash{}, (3) A JSON object can be converted to C++ associative containers such as {\ttfamily std\+::unordered\+\_\+map\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}std\+::string\textbackslash{}, json\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}.,operator\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Value\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{a00650__deprecated000005}{Deprecated}}]This stream operator is deprecated since 3.\+0.\+0 and will be removed in version 4.\+0.\+0 of the library. Please use \doxylink{a01541_abfcb46247e0d5ec0a442c3193c5305be}{operator$>$$>$(std\+::istream\&, basic\+\_\+json\&)} instead; that is, replace calls like {\ttfamily j \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} i;} with {\ttfamily i \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} j;}. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{a00650__deprecated000003}{Deprecated}}]This function is deprecated since 3.\+0.\+0 and will be removed in version 4.\+0.\+0 of the library. Please use \doxylink{a01541_a5bbe57177fdb5833885dc1567ec13394}{operator$<$$<$(std\+::ostream\&, const basic\+\_\+json\&)} instead; that is, replace calls like {\ttfamily j \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} o;} with {\ttfamily o \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} j;}. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
